## Cement Sector Analysis

The Indian cement industry is a significant sector in the country's economy, with a market size of over INR 60,000 crores. The industry has experienced significant growth in recent years, driven by the government's infrastructure development initiatives and a surge in housing demand.

## Key Trends

* The top 5 players in the Indian cement industry account for over 50% of the market share.
* The industry is witnessing a consolidation trend, with larger players acquiring smaller ones to increase their market share.
* The demand for cement is expected to grow at a CAGR of 7-8% in the next 5 years, driven by the government's infrastructure development plans.

## Investment Opportunities
